<div id="review_3066623974" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3066623974" />
    <a title="Steve R" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/51602729-steve-r"><img alt="Steve R" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550608435p2/51602729.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steve R" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steve R" href="/user/show/51602729-steve-r">Steve R</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3066623974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5035570086675783656">This is one of the best Frank Herbert novels outside his Dune series. Unlike most of his works, it has a connection with real-life situations in the world of the 1980s. (It was published in 1982). The issue of Irish terrorism, of English suppression of Irish just demands and of Libyan support of international instability are all significant points in the developing plot, as a personal tragedy, combined with a peculiar expertise in biological manipulations allow for a truly harrowing situation to</span>
  <span id="freeText5035570086675783656" style="display:none">This is one of the best Frank Herbert novels outside his Dune series. Unlike most of his works, it has a connection with real-life situations in the world of the 1980s. (It was published in 1982). The issue of Irish terrorism, of English suppression of Irish just demands and of Libyan support of international instability are all significant points in the developing plot, as a personal tragedy, combined with a peculiar expertise in biological manipulations allow for a truly harrowing situation to develop in the three countries. Operating on personal, scientific, political and a global power levels, I found this not only thrilling to read, but also extremely thought provoking: my emotions were both with and against the protagonist, almost in equal measure and even at one and the same time. Truly a remarkable achievement for an author.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5035570086675783656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer47637847" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16078248891654471126">An interesting "end of the world" sci-fi novel, that deals with human caused disaster. Since it was one person that caused the disaster - sort of on purpose - we would probably call it a terrorist novel these days. But the novel delves into what happens when one person who tries to strike back at terrorists (the IRA in this case) goes tragically wrong. <br/><br/>I was not a big fan of Frank Herbet's Dune (I know blasphemy). But I loved this book. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2475741009" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2475741009" />
    <a title="John Loyd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3716161-john-loyd"><img alt="John Loyd" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475255722p2/3716161.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2475741009?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="John Loyd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="John Loyd" href="/user/show/3716161-john-loyd">John Loyd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2475741009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4095426307354017037">John Roe O'Neill is a molecular biologist. He is going to Ireland to work on a project there for an extended time. He hasn't been there long, just getting over the jet lag, when a car bomb kills his wife and children. He was watching from the bank manager's window when it happened. He is distraught. He goes home and seeks revenge. The plague he created is very contagious and fatal for women. Then symptoms for men are mild but they remain carriers. He has released the plague in the targets of his</span>
  <span id="freeText4095426307354017037" style="display:none">John Roe O'Neill is a molecular biologist. He is going to Ireland to work on a project there for an extended time. He hasn't been there long, just getting over the jet lag, when a car bomb kills his wife and children. He was watching from the bank manager's window when it happened. He is distraught. He goes home and seeks revenge. The plague he created is very contagious and fatal for women. Then symptoms for men are mild but they remain carriers. He has released the plague in the targets of his revenge, Ireland, England and Libya, but pockets of infection have spread throughout the world. <br /><br />He sent warning letters to leaders and media all over the globe saying the countries he was targeting, warning them not to sterilize the infected areas with atomics, he would release another plague. We follow John O'Neill/McCarthy/O'Donnell, the american president, a couple of groups battling the plague, one man and woman who took refuge in a decompression tank and a couple others. There is a lot of talk about using atomic weapons to wipe out the infection, but no talk of the mounting death toll. John O'Donnell makes it to plague filled Ireland and takes a months long trek with Herity, Father Michael and the Boy to make it to the lab. O'Neill's plan was to sabotage the effort for a cure. <br /><br />Herbert is asking for a great suspension of disbelief. The premise is that one man can create a plague that infects everyone, kills women and leaves men as carriers and is so virulent it's unstoppable. OK. Then we have to accept the governments are considering nuking the infected area into oblivion, finding a cure for themselves and not sharing. A trial of O'Neill, yes, but the defense argument is this was an act of war. Father Michael comparing the Madman's actions with the acts of "war" perpetrated by the Finn Sadal (aka the IRA). <br /><br />Darwin's Raido by Greg Bear is much better if you're looking for a novel using genetics as the main premise. If you're looking for a society that is collapsing, something like Bova's The Precipice makes more sense. This novel wasn't bad, but I never identified with any of the characters. Or if I did it was with O'Neill. So if they find a cure it's "Great, humanity is saved" and if they don't it's "Oh, well, at least O'Neill got his revenge." If there is such a thing as speed reading this is the ideal novel for it. Worth reading. I had heard of the IRA when I was a kid, but didn't really connect it with anything. This didn't go into the history of the IRA, but explained that there had been injustice going on for a long time. Maybe Herbert is telling us that the governments of 1982 were perceived as paranoid. There are so many other fantastic novels out there that I'm not going to recommend this one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4095426307354017037" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YzSjR+L9doMF8jCeaxIwUEvZyKYpKa1ER6VZmwPyKU63zXcUNadP0+MQYlwY3w4BplT/Xik7PgfG0Yue89zoww==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

Și alte eseuri despre simplitate<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/6570334.Valeriu_Gherghel?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Valeriu Gherghel<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p6\"><\/span><\/span> 4.74 avg rating &mdash; 19 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2012\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer17874802440788773220\">Principiul simplitatii sau al economiei i-a preocupat dintotdeauna pe filosofi si logicieni, care de-a lungul timpului au propus pentru el diferite formulari si interpretari. Eseurile lui Valeriu Gherghel sint centrate pe simplitatea aplicata in inte<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText17874802440788773220\" style=\"display:none\">Principiul simplitatii sau al economiei i-a preocupat dintotdeauna pe filosofi si logicieni, care de-a lungul timpului au propus pentru el diferite formulari si interpretari. Eseurile lui Valeriu Gherghel sint centrate pe simplitatea aplicata in interpretarea textelor, care presupune a nu fi excesiv, a respecta limita si masura, a accepta faptul incomod ca poti explica numai ceea ce poti explica si a te margini strict la ceea ce spune textul, fara sa construiesti ipoteze suplimentare. Pe parcursul volumului, speculatia alterneaza cu exercitiul practic – analiza de text – si, in citeva cazuri, cu exercitiul imaginativ. Daca prima parte vorbeste despre simplitate si conciziune, iar cea de-a doua despre principiul opus, reprezentat de risipa interpretativa si exces, partea a treia prezinta unele episoade din istoria hermeneuticii (Philon din Alexandria, Sfintul Augustin, Hugo de Saint-Victor) care demonstreaza cit este de dificil sa fii simplu in interpretare.\n \n„Istoria hermeneuticii e plina de exegeti dogmatici. Scepticii veritabili pot fi numarati pe degetele unei singure miini. In interpretare, toti pot sa poata. Si nimeni nu poate sa nu poata. Nu exista semnificatii tainuite, pagini abstruse, vid semantic, intuneric. E absolut uimitor acest dogmatism al criticilor. In teologie, e o distinctie si o trufie sa fii agnostic si sa-ti recunosti, inca de la debutul discutiei, ignoranta. Fiinta lui Dumnezeu e dincolo de patrunderea mintii. Aici, nestiinta e o virtute glorificata. In hermeneutica, dimpotriva. A marturisi ca nu intuiesti o semnificatie, ca sensul precis al unei sintagme este cu neputinta de sesizat e ca si cum ti-ai recunoaste un viciu abominabil. Esenta divina se sustrage tuturor. In schimb, semnificatia unei scrieri e in vazul si la cheremul oricui. Asa sa fie oare?” (Valeriu Gherghel)\n \nDin cuprins: Hexada simplitatii • Don Quijote c’est moi • Limba neo-adamica • Crux interpretum • Simplitate si pesti (sancta simplicitas) • Erezia determinarii       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/58.Frank_Herbert">About Frank Herbert</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/58.Frank_Herbert"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1591018335p3/58.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/58.Frank_Herbert">Frank Herbert
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
8,442
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10602408429141886177">Frank Herbert was a critically acclaimed and commercially successful American science fiction author.<br/><br/>He is best known for the novel <i>Dune</i> and its five sequels. The Dune saga, set in the distant future and taking place over millennia, dealt with themes such as human survival and evolution, ecology, and the intersection of religion, politics, and power, and is widely considered to be among the classi</span>
  <span id="freeText10602408429141886177" style="display:none">Frank Herbert was a critically acclaimed and commercially successful American science fiction author.<br /><br />He is best known for the novel <i>Dune</i> and its five sequels. The Dune saga, set in the distant future and taking place over millennia, dealt with themes such as human survival and evolution, ecology, and the intersection of religion, politics, and power, and is widely considered to be among the classics in the field of science fiction.<br /><br />He was the father of fellow author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/56.Brian_Herbert" title="Brian Herbert" rel="nofollow noopener">Brian Herbert</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10602408429141886177" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
